    CaptionML=[ENU=Purchase Order;
               ENG=Purchase Order];
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  mCompanyInformation.GET();
                  mCompanyInformation.CALCFIELDS(Picture);

                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.ReportImages(mImage, TRUE);
                END;

  DATASET

    { 1000000000;;DataItem;dPurchaseHeader   ;
               DataItemTable=Table38;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document Type,No.)
                                 WHERE(Document Type=CONST(Order));
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lFormatAddress@1000000000 : Codeunit 365;
                                BEGIN
                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.SetPurchaseHeader(dPurchaseHeader);

                                  mTitle := STRSUBSTNO(tTitle, FORMAT(dPurchaseHeader."Document Type"), dPurchaseHeader."No.");

                                  lFormatAddress.Company(mCompanyAddress, mCompanyInformation);
                                  lFormatAddress.PurchHeaderBuyFrom(mBuyFromAddress, dPurchaseHeader);
                                  lFormatAddress.PurchHeaderPayTo(mPayToAddress, dPurchaseHeader);
                                  lFormatAddress.PurchHeaderShipTo(mShipToAddress, dPurchaseHeader);

                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.ContactInformation(mBuyFromContact);
                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.CurrencyInformation(mCurrencyText, mCurrencyFactorText, mAmountText, mAmountInclVatText);
                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.Summary(mAmount, mAmountInclVat, mAmountInWordsText);

                                  mPurchaserText := mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.SalespersonPurchaserText();
                                  mPaymentTermsText := mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.PaymentTermsText();
                                  mPaymentMethodText := mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.PaymentMethodText();
                                  mShipmentMethodText := mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.ShipmentMethodText();
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1000000001;1;DataItem;dCopy            ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1..));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.FilterCopy(mCopies, dCopy);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.NextCopy(dCopy, mCopyText);
                                  mDocumentId := STRSUBSTNO(tDocumentId, dPurchaseHeader."Document Type", dPurchaseHeader."No.", dCopy.Number);
                                END;
                                 }

                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.LineInternalInformation(mShowInternalInformation);
                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.GetPurchaseLine(dPurchaseLine);

                                  //DOC OP9031 -
                                  IF (dPurchaseLine.Type = dPurchaseLine.Type::Item) THEN BEGIN
                                    IF NOT mItem.GET(dPurchaseLine."No.") THEN
                                      mItem.INIT;
                                    IF NOT mStyle.GET(dPurchaseLine."Style No.") THEN
                                      mStyle.INIT;
                                  END;
                                  //DOC OP9031 +
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=dPurchaseHeader;
               DataItemLink=Document Type=FIELD(Document Type),
                            Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
